(1) Students enrolled in Life Science degree posts may not use this course towards any program requirements.
(2) This course is intended for students who are pursuing programs in Health and Society.
If you are looking to pursue a program in the Department of Psychology and do not have grade 12 Biology
completed please enroll in BIOA12H3 instead.
If you are looking to pursue a program in the Department of Physical & Environmental Sciences that requires
BIOA01H3 and BIOA02H3 and do not have grade 12 Biology completed please enroll in BIOA12H3 instead.

BIOB98H3 (F) - Supervised Introductory Research in Biology
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a Supervised Study Form. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name, and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on
your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/biosci/undergraduate-research-opportunities
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form by email before the last day to add courses for the session.
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP)

BIOD95H3 (F) - Supervised Study in Biology
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a Supervised Study Form. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name, and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on
your transcript. The Supervised Study Form and Departmental Permission Forms are available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/biosci/undergraduate-research-opportunities
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email before the last day to add
courses for the session. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

number of practicals/tutorials currently open in some Fall/Winter courses does not accommodate all students
presently enrolled in them. This is deliberate because enrolment patterns change between registration dates and
the start of the term. When the term starts, if necessary, we will open additional practicals/tutorials to
accommodate the students enrolled in the course at that time.

CHMD90Y3 (Y) - Directed Research
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Contact the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name, and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on
your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form . Your Department listed below may require
additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and any additional paperwork by email to
dpes-undergrad.utsc@utoronto.ca. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to
approved (APP).

Advancing Your Career Exploration (AYCE) is a mandatory course for all Management Co-op students prior to
seeking for their first work-term. It is a credit requirement in addition to your BBA degree requirements and is not
included in your cGPA. There are no tuition fees attached to this course. AYCE will begin the first week of
classes.
For any questions regarding this class, please contact the Management Co-op office at 416.287.7111 or
mgmtcoop.utsc@utoronto.ca

COPB30H3 (F) - Passport to Placement Part I
Enrolment Indicator: E
Enrolment via ACORN is not available. Students must request permission to enrol in this course by
contacting the sponsoring department.
The International Development Studies Co-op Placement Preparation Course (COPB30) is mandatory for all
new students entering the co-op program. Students entering the program must take this course in their first year,
in the Fall term. For students entering in their second year, they must take this course in the Fall term of their
second year. This course is a prerequisite for COPB31. Students will automatically be enrolled in this course, but
must ensure their timetable is clear for this registration. It is non-credit with no tuition fees attached.
NOTE: Students are responsible for ensuring they understand coop course requirements, and that they do not
register for other courses during the time the coop course is offered. For any issues regarding the scheduling of
this course, please contact the IDS co-op office as soon as possible at 416-287-7113 or
ids-coop@utsc.utoronto.ca
Exclusion: COPD02H3
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor

courses each semester based on their program of study and co-op work term sequence. Students entering the
co-op program in 2021 onward will be required to enroll in the co-op course during their first year. Co-op courses
are offered each semester.

any questions regarding your enrolment please contact askcoop@utoronto.ca

Students who do not require this course for their program must meet additional Cumulative GPA (CGPA)
requirements:
* A student who is not in a CSC program and does not have a CGPA of at least 3.5 may not take any B- level
CSC course, with exception of CSCB20H3.
* A student who is not in a CSC program and does not have a CGPA of at least 3.5 may not take any C- or
D-level CSC course.
* When a B-, C-, or D-level CSC course approaches its capacity, CSC program students will be given preference
for further enrollment over non-CSC program students.
Refer to the computer science section of the calendar for more information on admission to courses.

accommodate all students enrolled in the course. Keep checking ACORN. More information will be provided
during the first class.

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Email the CMS faculty member and obtain their approval, make sure the course code, supervisor name,
and title of the project is input on the form as this information will appear on your transcript.
Step 3: Submit the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study form by email
to Kelly Squier kelly.squier@utoronto.ca
The department will arrange to have your course status on ACORN changed from interim (INT) to approved
(APP). The Supervised Study form is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form.
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork.

Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Contact the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name, and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on
your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form . Your Department listed below may require
additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and any additional paperwork by email to
dpes-undergrad.utsc@utoronto.ca.
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your
transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require
additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Step 3: Please submit any requests for access to this course course to eng-ugc.utsc@utoronto.ca where
requests will be reviewed. Students will either be contacted for more information or approved on Acorn from
interim (INT) to approved (APP).

FRED02H3 (F) - Supervised Reading
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Secure a faculty member you would be interested in working with as a supervisor for your project.
Step 2: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 3: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your
transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Students should contact the departmental office
listed for more information.
Step 4: Submit the fully completed and signed Supervised Study form by email to dls-ua@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor
LEC 1 INPER

code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your
transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require
additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information.

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Secure a faculty member as a supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Ensure
the course code, supervisor's name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will
appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Sean Ramrattan sean.ramrattan@utoronto.ca one
week prior to the last day to add courses for the session. Staff will ensure your course status on ACORN will be
updated from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

IDSB10H3 (F) - Political Economy of Knowledge Technology and Development
Open to all UTSC students. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on 6:00am on August 6, 2025.

Course Description: How is artificial intelligence shaping us, and who is engineering our futures
AI tools like ChatGPT, Zoom, and Canvas have become everyday platforms, yet they carry hidden assumptions
about knowledge, labour, and power that often go unexamined. This course critically explores how AI is
reshaping education, economic growth, and global inequality, raising urgent questions around data governance,
techno-nationalism, and algorithmic justice and what they mean for development.
We will examine how digital infrastructures determine what counts as knowledge and whose interests they serve.
Topics include algorithmic governance, platform capitalism, the geopolitics of AI, and Indigenous approaches to
technology and sovereignty. Anchored in global and community contexts, we will explore how diverse groups
resist, redesign, and reimagine technological systems.
Through case studies, media analysis, and collaborative mapping, students will explore strategies for asserting
individual and collective agency, challenging extractive and inequitable systems, and imagining alternative AI
futures grounded in justice, care, and epistemic pluralism.
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor
LEC 1 TH 13:00 - 15:00 INPER Chan, L.

LEC 1 MO 13:00 - 15:00 INPER Ilmi, A.

IDSC16H3 (F) - Populism, Development, and Globalization in the Global South
Open to all UTSC students. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on 6:00am on August 6, 2025.
Course Description: This course examines the emergence of movements and regimes labelled as “populist,” with
particular attention to the differing impacts of economic globalization on the social, economic and political
conditions of countries of the Global South and Global North. The course draws attention to the substantive
differences among cases and their impacts, raising the question of the usefulness of the populist label. Case
studies include Trump (US), Bolsonaro (Brazil), Chavez (Venezuela), and Modi (India).

IDSD19H3 (F) - The Role of Researcher- Practitioner Engagement in Development
Open to all UTSC students. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on 6:00am on August 6, 2025.
Course Description: This course focuses on training students in community-based participatory research. This
course is designed in partnership with the Toronto-based non-profit organization Volunteer Toronto
(www.volunteertoronto.ca). Students will participate in a research project for Volunteer Toronto. Throughout the
course students will explore whether community-based participatory research offers opportunities for effective
social change.

[1] You do need to take the placement/survey if you have never done so before.
[2] In general, there is NO need to take the test/survey again.
[3] Please do not email any instructor after you have successfully submitted your test/survey.
[4] The instructors will receive an automatic email alert.
[5] You will receive notification from an instructor within two business days regarding your status in the course.
Your status on ACORN should be updated within 10 days of this notification.
[6] Students are welcome to select these courses but will not be officially enrolled until approved.
[7] Students whose level of proficiency in the language is considered unsuitable for the course will not be
permitted to take the course.
[8] Students are not permitted to take LGGA- and LGGB-level courses in an incorrect sequence (i.e., take a
lower level course after a higher level course). Click a specific course code to read the description, including the
Exclusion.

[2] In general, there is NO need to take the test/survey again.
[3] Please do not email any instructor after you have successfully submitted your test/survey.
[4] The instructors will receive an automatic email alert.
[5] You will receive notification from an instructor within two business days regarding your status in the course.
Your status on ACORN should be updated within 10 days of this notification.
[6] Students are welcome to select these courses but will not be officially enrolled until approved.
[7] Students whose level of proficiency in the language is considered unsuitable for the course will not be
permitted to take the course.
[8] Students are not permitted to take LGGA- and LGGB-level courses in an incorrect sequence (i.e., take a
lower level course after a higher level course). Click a specific course code to read the description, including the
Exclusion.

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Secure a faculty member you would be interested in working with as a supervisor for your project.
Step 2: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 3: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your
transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require
additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information.
Submit the fully completed and signed Supervised Study form by email to dls-ua@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

MATD92H3 (F) - Mathematics Project
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Email the CMS faculty member and obtain their approval, make sure the course code, supervisor name,
and title of the project is input on the form as this information will appear on your transcript.
Step 3: Submit the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study form by email
to Kelly Squier kelly.squier@utoronto.ca
The department will arrange to have your course status on ACORN changed from interim (INT) to approved
(APP). The Supervised Study form is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form.
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork.
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor

MANAGEMENT MEETING SECTION CHANGES: Students approved in a course who wish to change sections
may do so on ACORN, provided there is space in the preferred section. Note: if the preferred section is full and
you add yourself to the waitlist, your enrolment in the original section will be cancelled. Section changes can be
made on ACORN until the last day to add courses for the session provided there is space to do so.
Students are expected to enroll or waitlist for course meeting sections that fit in a conflict-free schedule. Students
who knowingly enroll in a course that causes a conflict should not expect to request a section change through
their Professor at a later date.

SCSPE01332 - Specialist (Co-operative) Program in Economics for Management Studies
Visiting students require the permission of the Academic Director.
MANAGEMENT MEETING SECTION CHANGES: Students approved in a course who wish to change sections
may do so on ACORN, provided there is space in the preferred section. Note: if the preferred section is full and
you add yourself to the waitlist, your enrolment in the original section will be cancelled. Section changes can be
made on ACORN until the last day to add courses for the session provided there is space to do so.
Students are expected to enroll or waitlist for course meeting sections that fit in a conflict-free schedule. Students
who knowingly enroll in a course that causes a conflict should not expect to request a section change through
their Professor at a later date.
Please see Calendar for overall course load limit for BBA students

SCSPE01332 - Specialist (Co-operative) Program in Economics for Management Studies
Enrolment will open to all UTSC students at 10:00am on July 23, 2025. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM
students on 6:00am on August 6, 2025.
Students not in the program, including Minors in Economics, ARE REQUIRED to have a CGPA of 2.0 or better if
they want to enroll in in MGEB02H3, MGEB06H3, MGEB11H3, MGEB12H3, MGEC02H3, MGEC06H3, and
MGEC11H3.
BBA students are no longer allowed to use STAB22H3 or STAB23H3 to fulfill program requirements and they will
be restricted from taking STAB22H3 and STAB23H3. BBA students who have completed STAB22H3 after
August 2012 or STAB23H3 ARE REQUIRED to take MGEB11H3 as EXTRA before enrolling themselves into
MGEB12H3
Which course will be open to Non-Program Students and When
Non-Program students (including Economics Minor students) may enroll in MGEA02H3, MGEA06H3 and
MGEC93H3 from the start of course enrolment.
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor
LEC 1 TU 14:00 - 17:00 INPER Cavenaile, L.

MGED90H3 (F) - Supervised Reading
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the MGE faculty member who you hope will supervise your study/project and obtain their
approval. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title of the project is input on the supervised study
form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form
Step 3: Once complete, send the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study
form by email to the Academic Director, Economics ecoss.utsc@utoronto.ca and Jacqueline Deane
jacqueline.deane@utoronto.ca
Step 4: If your proposal is approved, the department will update the Registrar's Office with your Supervised
Study form. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. See policy for more details: https://www.utsc.ut
oronto.ca/mgmt/sites/utsc.utoronto.ca.mgmt/files/docs/Departmental%20Policy%20on%20Supervised%20Readi
ng%20Courses%20(October%202023).pdf
Economics and Management Office IC250

Enrolment Indicator: R
Restricted to students in the following groups:
MGT - All Management Students
SCSPE0133 - Specialist Program in Economics for Management Studies
SCSPE01332 - Specialist (Co-operative) Program in Economics for Management Studies

Visiting students require the permission of the Academic Director.
MANAGEMENT MEETING SECTION CHANGES: Students approved in a course who wish to change sections
may do so on ACORN, provided there is space in the preferred section. Note: if the preferred section is full and
you add yourself to the waitlist, your enrolment in the original section will be cancelled. Section changes can be
made on ACORN until the last day to add courses for the session provided there is space to do so.
Students are expected to enroll or waitlist for course meeting sections that fit in a conflict-free schedule. Students
who knowingly enroll in a course that causes a conflict should not expect to request a section change through
their Professor at a later date.
Please see Calendar for overall course load limit for BBA students

MANAGEMENT MEETING SECTION CHANGES: Students approved in a course who wish to change sections
may do so on ACORN, provided there is space in the preferred section. Note: if the preferred section is full and
you add yourself to the waitlist, your enrolment in the original section will be cancelled. Section changes can be
made on ACORN until the last day to add courses for the session provided there is space to do so.
Students are expected to enroll or waitlist for course meeting sections that fit in a conflict-free schedule. Students
who knowingly enroll in a course that causes a conflict should not expect to request a section change through
their Professor at a later date.
Please see Calendar for overall course load limit for BBA students

MGTD80H3 (F) - Supervised Reading in Management
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the MGE faculty member who you hope will supervise your study/project and obtain their
approval. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title of the project is input on the supervised study
form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form .
Step 3: Once complete, send the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study
form by email to the Academic Director, Economics ecoss.utsc@utoronto.ca and Jacqueline Deane
jacqueline.deane@utoronto.ca
Step 4: If your proposal is approved, the department will update the Registrar's Office with your Supervised
Study form. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork.
Economics and Management Office IC250

MGTD82Y3 (Y) - Supervised Reading in Management
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the MGT faculty member who you hope will supervise your study/project and obtain their
approval. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title of the project is input on the supervised study
form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form
Step 3: Once complete, send the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study
form by email to the Academic Director, Management mgmtss.utsc@utoronto.ca and Jacqueline Deane
jacqueline.deane@utoronto.ca
Step 4: If your proposal is approved, the department will update the Registrar's Office with your Supervised
Study form. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. See policy for more details: https://www.utsc.ut
oronto.ca/mgmt/sites/utsc.utoronto.ca.mgmt/files/docs/Departmental%20Policy%20on%20Supervised%20Readi
ng%20Courses%20(October%202023).pdf

your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the MGT faculty member who you hope will supervise your study/project and obtain their
approval. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title of the project is input on the supervised study
form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form
Step 3: Once complete, send the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study
form by email to the Academic Director, Management mgmtss.utsc@utoronto.ca and Jacqueline Deane
jacqueline.deane@utoronto.ca
Step 4: If your proposal is approved, the department will update the Registrar's Office with your Supervised
Study form. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. See policy for more details: https://www.utsc.ut
oronto.ca/mgmt/sites/utsc.utoronto.ca.mgmt/files/docs/Departmental%20Policy%20on%20Supervised%20Readi
ng%20Courses%20(October%202023).pdf
Economics and Management Office IC250

MUZA60H3 (F) - Concert Band Ia
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)

Course enrolment in the following Music Performance course is by an interview. An interview sign-up sheet will
be sent to students closer to the beginning of an academic term. To be considered follow the steps below:
* Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be 'INT'.
* Attend a placement interview - normally held during the week before and during the first week of classes. For
more details please visit https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/acm/music-culture and view the FAQ link.
* Decisions will be updated on ACORN beginning Monday, September 8th for the Fall Term and Monday,
January 12th for the Winter term.
Please enrol in a course you have the prerequisite for. Approval will only be granted if student is enrolled in the
correct course.
Check your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused;
INT = no decision yet). If ACORN has not been updated contact the Instructor immediately.

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Music Program Director to obtain permission to enroll in this course. You will be asked to
choose a supervisor and then obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code,
supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your
transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Students should contact the Office listed for more
information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to the ACM program
manager, acm-pm@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with your Supervisor and obtain their virtual signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the
course code, supervisor name and title of the project are clearly printed on the form as this information will
appear on your transcript. Print off your ACORN transcripts, and have your supervisor(s) sign each page of your
transcript. The Form is available on the Psychology website at:
https://utoronto.sharepoint.com/sites/utsc-psychology/SitePages/UG_Research-Courses.aspx
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form to psych.academic.utsc@utoronto.ca by the posted deadline
found on the website above. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved
(APP).

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your
transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require
additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Please submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Jason Ferreira jason.ferreira@utoronto.ca.
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
In order to qualify for a Supervised Study course, students must locate a professor who will agree to supervise
the course, and then follow the steps outlined below.
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be interim (INT).
You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps.
Step 2: Fill the 'Student' section on a 'Supervised Study Form' available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form
Step 3: Once you fill-in the 'Student' section, contact your Supervisor and provide them with the form. Your
supervisor will complete their section and forward the form for departmental approval.
Step 4: Once the project is approved at the departmental level, the form will be submitted to the Registrar's
Office and your status on ACORN will be updated from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES

Step 2: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 3: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your
transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Students should contact the departmental office
listed for more information.
Step 4: Submit the fully completed and signed Supervised Study form by email to dls-ua@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Secure a faculty member you would be interested in working with as a supervisor for your project.
Step 2: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 3: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your
transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Students should contact the departmental office
listed for more information.
Step 4: Submit the fully completed and signed Supervised Study form by email to dls-ua@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with your Supervisor and obtain their virtual signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the
course code, supervisor name and title of the project are clearly printed on the form as this information will
appear on your transcript. The Form is available on the Psychology website at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/psych/research-courses
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form to psych.academic.utsc@utoronto.ca by the posted deadline
found on the website above. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved
(APP)..

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with your Supervisor and obtain their virtual signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the
course code, supervisor name and title of the project are clearly printed on the form as this information will
appear on your transcript. The Form is available on the Psychology website at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/psych/research-courses
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form to psych.academic.utsc@utoronto.ca by the posted deadline
found on the website above. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved
(APP).

information: https://utoronto.sharepoint.com/sites/utsc-psychology/SitePages/UG_D-level-Courses.aspx.

SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with your Supervisor and obtain their virtual signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the
course code, supervisor name and title of the project are clearly printed on the form as this information will
appear on your transcript. Print off your ACORN transcripts, and have your supervisor(s) sign each page of your
transcript. The Form is available on the Psychology website at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/psych/research-courses
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form to psych.academic.utsc@utoronto.ca by the posted deadline
found on the website above. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved
(APP).

STAD92H3 (F) - Readings in Statistics
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Email the CMS faculty member and obtain their approval, make sure the course code, supervisor name,
and title of the project is input on the form as this information will appear on your transcript.
Step 3: Submit the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study form by email
to Kelly Squier kelly.squier@utoronto.ca
The department will arrange to have your course status on ACORN changed from interim (INT) to approved
(APP). The Supervised Study form is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form.
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork.

VPAD14H3 (F) - Independent Studies in Arts Management
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your
transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require
additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to the ACM Program
Manager acm-pm@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

VPHC45H3 (F) - Seminar in Modern and Contemporary Art
Open to all UTSC students. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on 6:00am on August 6, 2025.
This special topics course will consider the work of contemporary artists across the globe who have addressed
difficult histories, memories of trauma, loss and longing, exile and displacement. It will ask how, through their
creative practices, artists have questioned history, either by revising, revisiting, or reordering it.

beyond this limit.

WSTD01H3 (F) - Independent Project in Women's and Gender Studies
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check
your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no
decision yet)
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you
complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name, and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on
your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department may require additional
paperwork. Students should contact the Office for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to
hcs.advising.utsc@utoronto.ca. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved
(APP).
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor
LEC 1 INPER
